# Data dictionary for the 2022 census tract-level files provided by `{censoBR}`



## Description

This file documents the content of the census tract-level aggregate files made available by the R package `{censoBR}` for the **2022 Demographic Census**. For more info on the package, check the [official GitHub page](https://ipeagit.github.io/censobr/). 

All census tract-level aggregate files were downloaded by the script `code/01-download-data.r`, which saves the datasets in parquet format in the `data/raw` folder with names in the format `2022_*.parquet`.

When available, the dictionary incorporates metadata from the dictionary provided by IBGE and from its Markdown transcription.

- The IBGE dictionary was downloaded by the `{censoBR}` package and stored in `docs/original/2022_dictionary_tracts.xlsx`.
- The Markdown transcription of the original dictionary is stored in `docs/2022_dictionary_tracts.md`.

When metadata are not available in those files, this is explicitly indicated.

This data dictionary was generated by Pedro H. G. Ferreira de Souza, with support from OpenAI Codex using GPT-5.5.

- Generated on: 2026-04-25
- Total documented files: 9



## Companion CSV Structure

The content of this data dictionary is mirrored in the companion file `docs/data_dictionaries/2022_censobr_data_dictionary_eng.csv`.

This CSV file contains one row for each variable in each parquet file related to the census tract-level aggregates from the 2022 Census. That is, the combination of the `file_raw` and `column_name` columns provides unique identifiers for each row of the CSV file.

The CSV file contains the following columns:

- `file_raw`: exact name of the parquet file to which the row refers, such as `2022_Pessoas.parquet`.
- `dataset_name`: short name of the dataset derived from the file, such as `Pessoas`, `Basico`, or `Preliminares`.
- `column_name`: exact name of the column as it appears in the parquet file.
- `column_order`: position of the column in the parquet schema, indexed from 1.
- `type_parquet`: data type of the column in the parquet file, such as `string`, `double`, or `int32`.
- `source_sheet`: name of the workbook sheet used as the metadata source when available, such as `Basico`, `Domicilios`, or `Entorno`; blank when no sheet directly documents the variable.
- `source_name_original`: original name or code of the variable in the source documentation, such as `CD_SETOR`, `AREA_KM2`, or `V00644`.
- `theme`: thematic grouping of the variable in the documentation.
- `label_pt`: short Portuguese label of the variable, used as the main description in the dictionary.
- `categories`: categories or value labels when the documentation provides that information; blank when no categories are associated.
- `coverage_notes`: note about the universe of tracts and the coverage of the file to which the column belongs.
- `key_role`: functional role of the column in the dataset, such as `primary_key`, `geo_id`, `descriptor`, or `measure`.
- `join_key`: indicates whether the column can be used as a join key, with values such as `yes`, `no`, or `possible`.
- `present_in_workbook_dict`: indicates whether the variable is documented, for that specific file, in the dictionary derived from the Excel workbook.
- `present_in_md_dict`: indicates whether the variable is documented, for that specific file, in the source Markdown dictionary or in its geographic identification section.
- `notes`: free-text field for observations, caveats, name differences, reused metadata, inferences, or specific documentation issues.

The `present_in_workbook_dict` and `present_in_md_dict` fields indicate whether the variable is documented for that specific raw file, not merely whether a column with the same name exists in another workbook sheet or another Markdown section. Therefore, in `2022_Preliminares.parquet`, columns such as `code_tract` and `code_muni` appear with `source_sheet = Basico` because metadata were reused, but remain marked as `present_in_workbook_dict = no` and `present_in_md_dict = no`.



## Overview of Parquet Files

| File                       | Dataset          | Rows | Unique tracts | Duplicates | Columns | Documented in workbook? |
| ----------------------------- | ---------------- | -----: | -------------: | ---------: | ------: | ------------------------ |
| 2022_Basico.parquet           | Basico           | 468099 |         468099 |          0 |      36 | yes                      |
| 2022_Domicilio.parquet        | Domicilio        | 458772 |         458772 |          0 |     672 | yes                      |
| 2022_Entorno.parquet          | Entorno          | 344841 |         344841 |          0 |     134 | yes                      |
| 2022_Indigenas.parquet        | Indigenas        | 458772 |         458772 |          0 |    1058 | yes                      |
| 2022_Obitos.parquet           | Obitos           | 458772 |         458772 |          0 |     122 | yes                      |
| 2022_Pessoas.parquet          | Pessoas          | 458772 |         458772 |          0 |     704 | yes                      |
| 2022_Preliminares.parquet     | Preliminares     | 452340 |         452340 |          0 |      29 | no                       |
| 2022_Quilombolas.parquet      | Quilombolas      | 458772 |         458772 |          0 |     980 | yes                      |
| 2022_ResponsavelRenda.parquet | ResponsavelRenda | 458772 |         458772 |          0 |      34 | yes                      |

**Notes:**

- The files are in `data/raw/`.
- The `Unique tracts` and `Duplicates` columns use the `code_tract` variable as reference.
- The `Documented in workbook?` column indicates whether the file is listed in the Excel workbook `docs/original/2022_dictionary_tracts.xlsx`.



## Dictionary by File

### 2022_Basico.parquet

- Dataset: `Basico`
- Rows: `468099`
- Unique tracts (`code_tract`): `468099`
- `code_tract` duplicates: `0`
- Columns: `36`
- Source workbook sheet: `Basico`
- Coverage: Basic universe with 468099 unique tracts and no `code_tract` duplicates. Includes 9327 tracts absent from the six thematic files with 458772 rows.
- Note: Documented by the `Basico` sheet of the 2022 workbook.

### 2022_Pessoas.parquet

- Dataset raw: `Pessoas`
- Rows: `458772`

- `code_tract` duplicates: `0`
- Columns: `704`
- Source workbook sheet: `Pessoas`
- Coverage: Thematic universe with 458772 unique tracts and no `code_tract` duplicates. Same set of tracts in `Pessoas`, `Domicilio`, `Obitos`, `Indigenas`, `Quilombolas`, and `ResponsavelRenda`; subset of `Basico`.
- Note: The column order in the parquet differs from the workbook/md order: after `alfabetizacao_V01005`, the parquet places the `raca_*` block before `demografia_*` and `parentesco_*`.

### 2022_Domicilio.parquet

- Dataset raw: `Domicilio`
- Rows: `458772`
- Unique tracts (`code_tract`): `458772`
- `code_tract` duplicates: `0`
- Columns: `672`
- Source workbook sheet: `Domicilios`
- Coverage: Thematic universe with 458772 unique tracts and no `code_tract` duplicates. Same set of tracts in `Pessoas`, `Domicilio`, `Obitos`, `Indigenas`, `Quilombolas`, and `ResponsavelRenda`; subset of `Basico`.
- Note: The parquet file uses the singular name `Domicilio`, while the source spreadsheet/documentation uses `Domicilios`.

|Order|Column|Parquet type|Theme|Original name|Description|Categories|Role|Join key|
|-:|-|-|-|-|-|-|-|-|
|1|code_tract|string|Identificação Geográfica|CD_SETOR|Geocódigo de Setor Censitário||primary_key|yes|
|2|situacao|string|Identificação Geográfica|SITUACAO|Situação do Setor Censitário|Urbana; Rural|descriptor|no|
|3|code_situacao|double|Identificação Geográfica|CD_SIT|Situação detalhada do Setor Censitário|1 = Área urbana de alta densidade de edificações de cidade ou vila; 2 = Área urbana de baixa densidade de edificações de cidade ou vila; 3 = Núcleo urbano; 5 = Aglomerado rural - Povoado; 6 = Aglomerado rural - Núcleo rural; 7 = Aglomerado rural - Lugarejo; 8 = Área rural (exclusive aglomerados); 9 = Massas de água|descriptor|no|
|4|code_type|double|Identificação Geográfica|CD_TIPO|Tipo do Setor Censitário|0 = Não especial; 1 = Favela e Comunidade Urbana; 2 = Quartel e base militar; 3 = Alojamento / acampamento; 4 = Setor com baixo patamar domiciliar; 5 = Agrupamento indígena; 6 = Unidade prisional; 7 = Convento / hospital / ILPI / IACA; 8 = Agrovila do PA; 9 = Agrupamento quilombola|descriptor|no|

### 2022_Obitos.parquet

- Dataset raw: `Obitos`
- Rows: `458772`
- Unique tracts (`code_tract`): `458772`
- `code_tract` duplicates: `0`
- Columns: `122`
- Source workbook sheet: `Obitos`
- Coverage: Thematic universe with 458772 unique tracts and no `code_tract` duplicates. Same set of tracts in `Pessoas`, `Domicilio`, `Obitos`, `Indigenas`, `Quilombolas`, and `ResponsavelRenda`; subset of `Basico`.

### 2022_Quilombolas.parquet

- Dataset raw: `Quilombolas`
- Rows: `458772`
- Unique tracts (`code_tract`): `458772`
- `code_tract` duplicates: `0`
- Columns: `980`
- Source workbook sheet: `Quilombolas`
- Coverage: Thematic universe with 458772 unique tracts and no `code_tract` duplicates. Same set of tracts in `Pessoas`, `Domicilio`, `Obitos`, `Indigenas`, `Quilombolas`, and `ResponsavelRenda`; subset of `Basico`.
- Note: Documented by the `Quilombolas` sheet of the 2022 workbook.

|Order|Column|Parquet type|Theme|Original name|Description|Categories|Role|Join key|
|-:|-|-|-|-|-|-|-|-|
|1|code_tract|string|Identificação Geográfica|CD_SETOR|Geocódigo de Setor Censitário||primary_key|yes|
|2|situacao|string|Identificação Geográfica|SITUACAO|Situação do Setor Censitário|Urbana; Rural|descriptor|no|
|3|code_situacao|double|Identificação Geográfica|CD_SIT|Situação detalhada do Setor Censitário|1 = Área urbana de alta densidade de edificações de cidade ou vila; 2 = Área urbana de baixa densidade de edificações de cidade ou vila; 3 = Núcleo urbano; 5 = Aglomerado rural - Povoado; 6 = Aglomerado rural - Núcleo rural; 7 = Aglomerado rural - Lugarejo; 8 = Área rural (exclusive aglomerados); 9 = Massas de água|descriptor|no|
|4|code_type|double|Identificação Geográfica|CD_TIPO|Tipo do Setor Censitário|0 = Não especial; 1 = Favela e Comunidade Urbana; 2 = Quartel e base militar; 3 = Alojamento / acampamento; 4 = Setor com baixo patamar domiciliar; 5 = Agrupamento indígena; 6 = Unidade prisional; 7 = Convento / hospital / ILPI / IACA; 8 = Agrovila do PA; 9 = Agrupamento quilombola|descriptor|no|

### 2022_Preliminares.parquet

- Dataset raw: `Preliminares`
- Rows: `452340`
- Unique tracts (`code_tract`): `452340`
- `code_tract` duplicates: `0`
- Columns: `29`
- Source workbook sheet: `não existe`
- Coverage: Preliminary universe with 452340 unique tracts and no `code_tract` duplicates. Parquet file is not documented in the workbook with the IBGE dictionary; universe differs from `Basico` and is not its subset.
- Note: File present in `data/raw/` but absent from workbook `docs/original/2022_dictionary_tracts.xlsx` and markdown `docs/2022_dictionary_tracts.md`.
- Observação adicional: as colunas compartilhadas com outros arquivos reaproveitam metadados de variáveis homônimas já documentadas; `code_micro`, `name_micro`, `code_meso` e `name_meso` foram descritas por inferência a partir do próprio parquet.
